# EDIFACT Transaction Sets APERAK-IFTRIN
This topic lists the EDIFACT transaction sets that are supported by BizTalk Server.  
  
 The following transaction sets are contained in this topic:  
  
-   [Transaction Sets APERAK-BMISRM](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#aperak)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets BOPBNK-CLASET](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#bopbnk)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets CNTCND-CONAPW](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cntcnd)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets CONDPV-CONWQD](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#condpv)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets COPARN-CREMUL](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#coparn)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets CUSCAR-DEBREC](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cuscar)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets DELFOR-DOCADV](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#delfor)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets DOCAMA-FINSTA](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#docama)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets GENRAL-IFTIAG](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#genral)  
  
-   [Transaction Sets IFTICL-IFTRIN](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#ifticl)  
  
##  <a name="aperak"></a> Transaction Sets APERAK-BMISRM

##  <a name="cntcnd"></a> Transaction Sets CNTCND-CONAPW
